! Title: AyushNix Search Cleaner List
! Description: A filter list which removes bullshit domains from search results and blocks them
! Expires: 1 day
! License: https://spdx.org/licenses/ISC.html
! Repo: https://github.com/ayushnix/adblock

! This list serves two purposes
! - remove bullshit domains from search engine results
! - block these bullshit domains

google.*##.g:has(a[href*="360wiki.ru"])
duckduckgo.com##a[href*="360wiki.ru"]:upward(4)
html.duckduckgo.com##a[href*="360wiki.ru"]:upward(.result)
lite.duckduckgo.com##a[href*="360wiki.ru"]:upward(tr)
lite.duckduckgo.com##a[href*="360wiki.ru"]:upward(tr)+tr
lite.duckduckgo.com##a[href*="360wiki.ru"]:upward(tr)+tr+tr
lite.duckduckgo.com##a[href*="360wiki.ru"]:upward(tr)+tr+tr+tr
millionshort.com##a[href*="360wiki.ru"]:upward(li)
search.brave.com###results > div:has(a[href*="360wiki.ru"])
yandex.com##a[href*="360wiki.ru"]:upward(li)
www.bing.com##a[href*="360wiki.ru"]:upward(li)
startpage.com##.w-gl__result:has(a[href*="360wiki.ru"])
ecosia.org##.result:has(a[href*="360wiki.ru"])
360wiki.ru
